============================================================
MANUAL 06

CONTENT WRITING & EDUCATIONAL STANDARDS

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official standards for creating, reviewing, translating, and maintaining educational content inside Night Gym Academy.

Its purpose is to ensure that every lesson, article, exercise, anatomy page, nutrition guide, examination, and AI-generated explanation follows the same educational philosophy and quality standards.

Educational content is the heart of Night Gym Academy.

Every word matters.

============================================================
1. CONTENT PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Educational content should always be:

Accurate

Simple

Professional

Evidence-Based

Up-to-Date

Practical

Student-Centered

The objective is not to impress students.

The objective is to help them understand.

============================================================
2. WRITING STYLE
============================================================

Content should be:

Clear

Logical

Friendly

Professional

Direct

Easy to Read

Avoid unnecessary technical jargon.

Introduce advanced terminology gradually.

============================================================
3. TARGET AUDIENCE
============================================================

Every lesson should identify its audience.

Examples

Beginner

Intermediate

Advanced

Coach

Medical Student

Sports Science Student

Professional Trainer

Content difficulty should match the audience.

============================================================
4. LESSON STRUCTURE
============================================================

Every lesson should follow this structure:

Title

Learning Objectives

Introduction

Main Content

Examples

Practical Applications

Common Mistakes

Summary

Key Points

Quiz

References

A consistent structure improves learning.

============================================================
5. EXPLANATION STYLE
============================================================

Explain concepts using:

Simple Language

Step-by-Step Logic

Real-Life Examples

Visual Descriptions

Comparisons

Analogies

Complex ideas should become understandable.

============================================================
6. SCIENTIFIC ACCURACY
============================================================

Every scientific statement should be:

Evidence-Based

Current

Verified

Referenced

Avoid myths.

Avoid bro-science.

Avoid unsupported claims.

============================================================
7. REFERENCES
============================================================

Whenever appropriate, educational content should reference:

Peer-Reviewed Research

Scientific Journals

International Guidelines

Recognized Textbooks

Professional Organizations

References improve credibility.

============================================================
8. EXERCISE CONTENT
============================================================

Every exercise page should include:

Exercise Name

Scientific Name

Difficulty

Equipment

Primary Muscles

Secondary Muscles

Technique

Breathing

Range of Motion

Common Mistakes

Coaching Tips

Variations

Alternatives

Safety Notes

============================================================
9. ANATOMY CONTENT
============================================================

Every anatomy page should include:

Muscle Name

Origin

Insertion

Innervation

Blood Supply

Function

Actions

Synergists

Antagonists

Clinical Notes

Exercises

Stretching

Scientific References

============================================================
10. NUTRITION CONTENT
============================================================

Nutrition pages should include:

Food Description

Calories

Macronutrients

Micronutrients

Serving Size

Health Benefits

Scientific Notes

Practical Advice

Warnings

References

============================================================
11. QUESTION WRITING
============================================================

Questions should:

Measure understanding.

Avoid ambiguity.

Avoid trick questions.

Include explanations.

Reference educational objectives.

Every question teaches something.

============================================================
12. EXAM STANDARDS
============================================================

Examinations should:

Measure competence.

Cover learning objectives.

Balance difficulty.

Remain fair.

Provide meaningful feedback.

Assessments support learning.

============================================================
13. LANGUAGE QUALITY
============================================================

Every page should be:

Proofread

Grammar Checked

Spell Checked

Consistent

Professional

Language quality reflects platform quality.

============================================================
14. TRANSLATIONS
============================================================

Translations should preserve:

Meaning

Scientific Accuracy

Terminology

Educational Intent

Never translate literally when meaning would be lost.

============================================================
15. VISUAL CONTENT
============================================================

Images should:

Support learning.

Be scientifically accurate.

Remain high quality.

Match the lesson.

Avoid unnecessary decoration.

Visuals should teach.

============================================================
16. ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Educational content should support:

Screen Readers

Alternative Text

Captions

Clear Headings

Readable Typography

Simple Navigation

Education should be accessible to everyone.

============================================================
17. AI-GENERATED CONTENT
============================================================

AI-generated content must always be:

Reviewed

Verified

Scientifically Checked

Edited

Approved

AI assists writers.

It does not replace expert review.

============================================================
18. CONTENT REVIEW PROCESS
============================================================

Draft

↓

Scientific Review

↓

Editorial Review

↓

Grammar Review

↓

Translation (If Needed)

↓

Quality Assurance

↓

Publication

Every published lesson should pass this workflow.

============================================================
19. CONTENT MAINTENANCE
============================================================

Review educational content regularly.

Update:

Research

Guidelines

Recommendations

Terminology

Images

References

Educational content should never become outdated.

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Every lesson should answer one question:

"Will the student understand this better after reading it?"

If the answer is yes,

the lesson is successful.

If the answer is no,

improve the lesson before publishing.

Night Gym Academy exists to create understanding—not simply information.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 06

MANUAL 07

UI / UX DESIGN STANDARDS

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official User Interface (UI) and User Experience (UX) standards for Night Gym Academy.

Every screen, interaction, animation, navigation pattern, layout, and visual element must follow these standards.

The objective is to create one consistent, premium educational experience across the entire platform.

A student should always feel confident, comfortable, and focused while learning.

============================================================
1. DESIGN PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

The design should always be:

Professional

Minimal

Premium

Modern

Elegant

Educational

Accessible

Consistent

Every design decision should improve learning.

============================================================
2. USER EXPERIENCE PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Users should never ask:

"Where do I click?"

"What should I do next?"

Every interface should naturally guide the user.

Learning should feel effortless.

============================================================
3. DESIGN PRINCIPLES
============================================================

Every interface should emphasize:

Clarity

Consistency

Hierarchy

Feedback

Accessibility

Performance

Simplicity

Predictability

The simplest solution is usually the best solution.

============================================================
4. VISUAL IDENTITY
============================================================

Night Gym Academy should feel like:

Premium Software

Not a Blog

Not a WordPress Theme

Not a Generic Dashboard

Not a Social Media App

The platform should immediately communicate professionalism.

============================================================

============================================================

Primary Background

Dark

Secondary Background

Dark Surface

Accent

Neon Green

or

Cyber Yellow

Danger

Red

Success

Green

Warning

Blue

6. TYPOGRAPHY

Heading 1

Heading 2

Caption

Label

Button Text

============================================================
7. SPACING SYSTEM
============================================================

Use consistent spacing.

Small

Medium

Large

Extra Large

Whitespace is an important design element.

Avoid crowded layouts.

============================================================
8. GRID SYSTEM
============================================================

Every page should follow a consistent layout grid.

Columns

Rows

Margins

Padding

Alignment

============================================================
9. NAVIGATION
============================================================

Navigation should always be:

Simple

Consistent

Visible

Predictable

Support:

Desktop

Tablet

Mobile

RTL

LTR

10. BUTTONS
============================================================

Buttons should communicate importance.

Primary

Main Action

Secondary

Alternative Action

Text

Minor Action

Danger

Destructive Action

============================================================
11. FORMS
============================================================

Forms should be:

Simple

Readable

Validated

Accessible

Helpful

Provide:

Labels

Placeholders

Validation

Error Messages

Success Messages

Users should never guess what is required.

============================================================
12. FEEDBACK
============================================================

Always provide feedback.

Examples

Loading

Success

Warning

Error

Empty State

Progress

The interface should communicate system status.

============================================================
13. ANIMATIONS
============================================================

Animations should be:

Smooth

Fast

Meaningful

Subtle

Examples

Fade

Slide

Scale

Hover

Animations should support—not distract from—the experience.

============================================================
14. RESPONSIVE DESIGN
============================================================

Every page should work on:

Desktop

Laptop

Tablet

Mobile

Portrait

Landscape

Responsive behavior is mandatory.

============================================================
15. ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Support:

Keyboard Navigation

Screen Readers

Visible Focus

Alternative Text

Accessible Colors

Readable Typography

Accessibility is part of good design.

============================================================
16. EDUCATIONAL UX
============================================================

Educational interfaces should encourage:

Reading

Understanding

Practice

Revision

Knowledge Retention

The interface should support learning psychology.

============================================================
17. DASHBOARD DESIGN
============================================================

Dashboards should display:

Progress

Goals

Recommendations

Statistics

Quick Actions

The dashboard should motivate students.

============================================================
18. ERROR EXPERIENCE
============================================================

When something fails:

Explain what happened.

Explain why.

Suggest a solution.

Allow retry.

Never blame the user.

============================================================
19. MICROINTERACTIONS
============================================================

Microinteractions include:

Hover Effects

Button Feedback

Loading States

Notifications

Completion Animations

============================================================
20. DESIGN REVIEW
============================================================

Before approving any interface, verify:

Consistency

Accessibility

Performance

Educational Value

Visual Hierarchy

Responsive Design

Readability

Professional Appearance

============================================================
21. FUTURE DESIGN FEATURES
============================================================

Future UI improvements may include:

Future innovation should remain consistent with the design language.

============================================================
22. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

A beautiful interface attracts users.

An intuitive interface keeps users.

An educational interface changes lives.

Every design decision inside Night Gym Academy should help students focus less on the interface—

and more on learning.

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official DevOps, Infrastructure, Deployment, Monitoring, and Operational Engineering standards for Night Gym Academy.

Its purpose is to ensure that the platform remains secure, scalable, highly available, observable, maintainable, and ready to support millions of users worldwide.

Infrastructure should never become a bottleneck for growth.

============================================================
1. DEVOPS PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Infrastructure should be:

Reliable

Scalable

Automated

Observable

Secure

Recoverable

Cost Efficient

Infrastructure exists to support developers and users.

============================================================

MANUAL 09

CYBERSECURITY & INFORMATION SECURITY HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Cybersecurity and Information Security standards for Night Gym Academy.

Security is a fundamental requirement—not an optional feature.

Every developer, architect, DevOps engineer, AI assistant, content administrator, and future contributor must follow these standards.

The objective is to protect:

Users

Educational Data

Certificates

Payments

Infrastructure

AI Systems

Business Assets

============================================================
1. SECURITY PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Security is everyone's responsibility.

Every system should be designed using the principle:

Secure By Design

Security should be considered before implementation,

not after deployment.

============================================================
2. SECURITY PRINCIPLES
============================================================

Confidentiality

Integrity

Availability

Accountability

Least Privilege

Defense In Depth

Zero Trust

These principles guide every security decision.

============================================================
3. USER ACCOUNT SECURITY
============================================================

Every account should support:

Strong Password Policy

Email Verification

Password Recovery

Session Expiration

Account Lockout

Future Multi-Factor Authentication

User identity should always be protected.

============================================================
4. PASSWORD POLICY
============================================================

Passwords should:

Never be stored in plain text.

Always be hashed.

Meet minimum complexity requirements.

Support password reset.

Never be logged.

Never be transmitted insecurely.

============================================================
5. AUTHENTICATION
============================================================

Authentication should verify:

Identity

Credentials

Session

Token Validity

Authentication failures should be logged.

============================================================
6. AUTHORIZATION
============================================================

Every request should verify:

Role

Permissions

Ownership

Subscription

Resource Access

Never trust client-side permissions.

============================================================
7. ROLE-BASED ACCESS CONTROL
============================================================

Example Roles

Guest

Student

Parent

Coach

Instructor

Moderator

Administrator

Super Administrator

Founder

Every role receives only the permissions it requires.

============================================================
8. DATA PROTECTION
============================================================

Protect:

Personal Information

Certificates

Exam Results

Payments

Messages

Learning Progress

Sensitive data should always be encrypted where appropriate.

============================================================
9. INPUT VALIDATION
============================================================

Validate every input.

Examples

Forms

API Requests

Uploads

Search

Filters

Parameters

Never trust user input.

============================================================
10. FILE UPLOAD SECURITY
============================================================

Validate:

Extension

MIME Type

Maximum Size

Virus Scan (Future)

Storage Location

File Name

Reject unsafe uploads immediately.

============================================================
11. API SECURITY
============================================================

Protect APIs using:

Authentication

Authorization

Rate Limiting

Input Validation

Logging

Monitoring

Versioning

APIs should expose only necessary information.

============================================================
12. DATABASE SECURITY
============================================================

Protect against:

SQL Injection

Unauthorized Access

Privilege Escalation

Backup Exposure

Credential Leakage

Use prepared statements and least privilege access.

============================================================
13. SESSION MANAGEMENT
============================================================

Sessions should support:

Expiration

Secure Cookies

Logout

Revocation

Device Tracking

Concurrent Session Control (Future)

Inactive sessions should expire automatically.

============================================================
14. ENCRYPTION
============================================================

Encrypt:

Passwords

Sensitive Data

API Communication

Backups

Secrets

Private Keys

Encryption should use modern industry standards.

============================================================
15. SECURITY LOGGING
============================================================

Log:

Authentication

Authorization Failures

Permission Changes

Payments

Certificate Issuance

Administrative Actions

Security Events

Logs should remain tamper-resistant.

============================================================
16. MONITORING
============================================================

Continuously monitor:

Failed Logins

Suspicious Activity

Server Health

API Abuse

Infrastructure

Database

AI Usage

Early detection reduces damage.

============================================================
17. INCIDENT RESPONSE
============================================================

Incident

↓

Detection

↓

Containment

↓

Investigation

↓

Recovery

↓

Documentation

↓

Lessons Learned

Every incident should strengthen security.

============================================================
18. BACKUP SECURITY
============================================================

Backups should be:

Encrypted

Verified

Offsite

Versioned

Regularly Tested

Backup access should be restricted.

============================================================
19. AI SECURITY
============================================================

Protect:

Prompt Data

Conversation History

Learning Records

Model Configuration

API Keys

AI systems should never expose confidential information.

============================================================
20. DEPENDENCY SECURITY
============================================================

Regularly review:

Frameworks

Libraries

Packages

SDKs

Operating Systems

Dependencies should remain updated.

============================================================
21. PRIVACY
============================================================

Respect user privacy.

Collect only necessary information.

Allow users to manage their data.

Provide transparent privacy policies.

Privacy builds trust.

============================================================
22. SECURITY TESTING
============================================================

Perform:

Static Analysis

Dynamic Analysis

Penetration Testing

Dependency Scanning

Configuration Review

Security Audits

Security should be tested continuously.

============================================================
23. COMPLIANCE
============================================================

Future compliance may include:

GDPR

CCPA

ISO 27001

SOC 2

Regional Privacy Regulations

Compliance should be planned from the beginning.

============================================================
24. FUTURE SECURITY FEATURES
============================================================

Future improvements include:

Multi-Factor Authentication

Passkeys

Hardware Security Keys

Biometric Authentication

Behavioral Analytics

Threat Intelligence

Zero Trust Network

AI Threat Detection

============================================================
25. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The strongest feature in Night Gym Academy is not AI.

It is not design.

It is not performance.

It is user trust.

Protecting that trust is the responsibility of every contributor.

Security is not a feature.

Security is a promise.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 09

MANUAL 10

SCIENTIFIC REVIEW & CONTENT VALIDATION HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official scientific review process for every educational resource inside Night Gym Academy.

Its purpose is to ensure that all educational material published on the platform is scientifically accurate, evidence-based, consistent, and professionally reviewed.

Scientific quality is one of the foundations of Night Gym Academy.

No educational content should be published without passing the review process defined in this manual.

============================================================
1. SCIENTIFIC PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Education should always be based on:

Evidence

Research

Professional Consensus

Verified Knowledge

Continuous Updates

Scientific integrity is more important than publishing speed.

============================================================
2. REVIEW OBJECTIVES
============================================================

The review process verifies:

Scientific Accuracy

Educational Quality

Grammar

Terminology

References

Visual Accuracy

Clinical Safety

Translation Quality

============================================================
3. REVIEW TEAM
============================================================

Educational Author

↓

Scientific Reviewer

↓

Medical Reviewer (When Applicable)

↓

Editor

↓

Translator (If Needed)

↓

Quality Assurance

↓

Publication

Every educational resource should follow this workflow.

============================================================
4. CONTENT TYPES
============================================================

The review process applies to:

Courses

Lessons

Exercise Library

Anatomy Library

Nutrition Library

Question Bank

Examinations

Certificates

Articles

AI Educational Responses

Scientific consistency should exist everywhere.

============================================================
5. SCIENTIFIC SOURCES
============================================================

Preferred sources include:

Peer-Reviewed Journals

International Guidelines

University Textbooks

Professional Organizations

Systematic Reviews

Meta-Analyses

Consensus Statements

Higher-quality evidence should always take priority.

============================================================
6. EVIDENCE HIERARCHY
============================================================

Highest Priority

Systematic Reviews

↓

Meta-Analyses

↓

Clinical Guidelines

↓

Randomized Controlled Trials

↓

Cohort Studies

↓

Case Studies

↓

Expert Opinion

↓

Personal Experience

Educational content should reflect the strongest available evidence.

============================================================
7. EXERCISE SCIENCE REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Technique

Range of Motion

Primary Muscles

Secondary Muscles

Equipment

Safety

Coaching Cues

Contraindications

Exercise information should remain practical and accurate.

============================================================
8. ANATOMY REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Muscle Names

Latin Terminology

Origin

Insertion

Innervation

Blood Supply

Actions

Synergists

Antagonists

Clinical Notes

Anatomical information should follow accepted international terminology.

============================================================
9. NUTRITION REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Calories

Macronutrients

Micronutrients

Serving Sizes

Dietary Recommendations

Supplement Information

Health Claims

Avoid unsupported nutritional claims.

============================================================
10. MEDICAL CONTENT
============================================================

Medical information should:

Remain educational.

Avoid diagnosis.

Avoid treatment recommendations beyond educational scope.

Encourage consultation with qualified healthcare professionals when appropriate.

============================================================
11. QUESTION BANK REVIEW
============================================================

Review:

Correct Answer

Distractors

Difficulty

Scientific Accuracy

Learning Objectives

Explanation

Questions should teach—not confuse.

============================================================
12. AI CONTENT REVIEW
============================================================

AI-generated educational content should be checked for:

Accuracy

Completeness

Bias

Scientific References

Terminology

Readability

AI content should never bypass human review.

============================================================
13. TRANSLATION REVIEW
============================================================

Scientific translations should preserve:

Meaning

Terminology

Context

Educational Intent

Avoid literal translation when scientific meaning would change.

============================================================
14. VISUAL REVIEW
============================================================

Review:

Muscle Diagrams

Exercise Images

Nutrition Graphics

Infographics

Animations

Labels

Visual content should support scientific understanding.

============================================================
15. VERSION CONTROL
============================================================

Every educational resource should record:

Version

Author

Scientific Reviewer

Approval Date

Revision History

Evidence evolves over time.

Documentation should evolve with it.

============================================================
16. UPDATE POLICY
============================================================

Educational resources should be reviewed:

After Major Scientific Updates

When Guidelines Change

When Errors Are Reported

On Scheduled Review Cycles

Knowledge should remain current.

============================================================
17. QUALITY CHECKLIST
============================================================

Before publication verify:

☐ Scientifically Accurate

☐ Educationally Clear

☐ Grammar Reviewed

☐ References Verified

☐ Images Reviewed

☐ Terminology Consistent

☐ Translation Reviewed

☐ Final Approval Granted

============================================================
18. CONFLICT RESOLUTION
============================================================

If scientific sources disagree:

Prefer:

Higher Quality Evidence

More Recent Evidence

Professional Consensus

International Guidelines

Document controversial topics clearly.

============================================================
19. FUTURE IMPROVEMENTS
============================================================

Future review enhancements may include:

Reference Database

Automated Citation Validation

AI Evidence Verification

Research Alerts

Medical Advisory Board

University Partnerships

Scientific Peer Review Network

Continuous scientific improvement should be encouraged.

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The reputation of Night Gym Academy depends on scientific trust.

Every lesson.

Every exercise.

Every anatomy page.

Every nutrition guide.

Every examination.

Every AI explanation.

should earn that trust through evidence, accuracy, and professional review.

Scientific excellence is not a feature.

It is the identity of Night Gym Academy.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 10

MANUAL 11

API DOCUMENTATION & OPENAPI STANDARDS

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official standards for documenting every API used by Night Gym Academy.

A well-designed API is only valuable if developers can easily understand and integrate with it.

API documentation should always remain synchronized with the implementation.

Documentation is part of the product—not an optional extra.

============================================================
1. API DOCUMENTATION PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

API documentation should be:

Complete

Accurate

Readable

Versioned

Maintainable

Searchable

Every endpoint should be understandable without reading the source code.

============================================================
2. DOCUMENTATION STANDARD
============================================================

Night Gym Academy should adopt:

OpenAPI Specification (OAS)

Version 3.x

Future documentation tools may include:

Swagger UI

Redoc

Postman Collections

Developer Portal

============================================================
3. EVERY ENDPOINT MUST INCLUDE
============================================================

Endpoint Name

Description

Purpose

HTTP Method

Authentication Requirements

Permissions

Parameters

Headers

Request Body

Response Body

Error Codes

Example Requests

Example Responses

Notes

Nothing should be undocumented.

============================================================

============================================================

GET

/api/v1/courses

Description

Retrieve all published courses.

Authentication

Optional

Parameters

page

limit

category

language

sort

Example Response

Course List

============================================================
5. REQUEST DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

Optional Fields

Allowed Values

Examples

============================================================
6. RESPONSE DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

Every response should define:

Structure

Field Definitions

Pagination

Metadata

Examples

============================================================

============================================================

Examples

Invalid Request

Forbidden

404

Not Found

409

Conflict

422

Validation Failed

500

Internal Error

Cause

Meaning

============================================================
8. AUTHENTICATION DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

Document:

Authentication Method

Token Type

Expiration

Refresh Process

Permissions

Protected Endpoints

Developers should easily authenticate.

============================================================
9. VERSIONING
============================================================

Every documented endpoint belongs to one API version.

Examples

v1

v2

v3

Breaking changes require new versions.

============================================================
10. CHANGELOG
============================================================

Every API modification should document:

Version

Date

Reason

Affected Endpoints

Migration Guide

Deprecation Notice

API evolution should remain transparent.

============================================================
11. EXAMPLES
============================================================

Every endpoint should provide:

Example Request

Example Response

Example Error

Example Authentication

Examples reduce developer confusion.

============================================================
12. PAGINATION
============================================================

Document:

Page

Limit

============================================================
13. FILTERING
============================================================

Document supported filters.

Examples

Difficulty

Language

Status

Instructor

Sorting

Filtering should follow one standard.

============================================================
14. WEBHOOKS (FUTURE)
============================================================

Examples

============================================================
15. SDK SUPPORT
============================================================

Future SDK documentation may include:

JavaScript

TypeScript

Flutter

Kotlin

Swift

Python

PHP

C#

============================================================
16. TESTING
============================================================

Every documented endpoint should be tested.

Documentation examples should always remain valid.

Broken examples reduce developer trust.

============================================================
17. INTERNAL APIs
============================================================

Internal services should also be documented.

Internal documentation is as important as public documentation.

============================================================
18. AI APIs
============================================================

Document:

Prompt Inputs

Context

Expected Outputs

Safety Rules

Rate Limits

Supported Models

AI integrations should remain predictable.

============================================================
19. DOCUMENTATION REVIEW
============================================================

Before publishing:

Verify Endpoint

Verify Errors

Verify Permissions

Verify Authentication

Verify Version

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The best API documentation answers every developer's question before they need to ask it.

If developers can successfully integrate without contacting the backend team,

the documentation has achieved its purpose.

MANUAL 12

SOFTWARE TESTING ENGINEERING HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official software testing standards for Night Gym Academy.

Testing ensures that every feature behaves correctly, remains secure, performs efficiently, and provides a reliable learning experience.

Quality is achieved through continuous testing—not by testing only before release.

============================================================
1. TESTING PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Testing should begin before coding.

Every feature should be designed to be testable.

Every bug should become a future test.

Testing reduces risk.

Testing protects quality.

Testing protects users.

============================================================
2. TESTING PYRAMID
============================================================

The recommended testing hierarchy:

Unit Tests

↓

Integration Tests

↓

API Tests

↓

UI Tests

↓

End-to-End Tests

↓

Manual Testing

Methods

Calculations

Business Rules

Validation

Examples

BMR Formula

it should not be released.

and quality begins with disciplined testing.

MANUAL 13

PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official performance engineering standards for Night Gym Academy.

Performance is one of the platform's core quality pillars.

A fast educational platform improves concentration, reduces frustration, increases learning efficiency, and improves accessibility.

Performance is a feature—not an afterthought.

============================================================
1. PERFORMANCE PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Every millisecond matters.

Every unnecessary request matters.

Every unnecessary render matters.

Every unnecessary query matters.

Performance should be considered from the first line of code.

============================================================
2. PERFORMANCE GOALS
============================================================

The platform should feel:

Fast

Responsive

Smooth

Reliable

Predictable

Educational content should appear immediately whenever possible.

============================================================
3. FRONTEND PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Optimize:

HTML

CSS

JavaScript

Fonts

Images

Icons

Animations

Rendering

Avoid unnecessary DOM operations.

============================================================
4. IMAGE OPTIMIZATION
============================================================

Use:

Modern Formats

Responsive Images

Lazy Loading

Compression

Proper Dimensions

Caching

Images should never be larger than necessary.

============================================================
5. VIDEO OPTIMIZATION
============================================================

Support:

Adaptive Streaming

Compression

Progressive Loading

Quality Selection

Caching

Poster Images

Educational videos should load efficiently.

============================================================
6. CSS PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Reduce:

Unused CSS

Duplicate Rules

Deep Selectors

Large Files

Prefer:

CSS Variables

Reusable Classes

Component-Based Styling

Clean CSS improves rendering.

============================================================
7. JAVASCRIPT PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Avoid:

Large Global Scope

Blocking Scripts

Duplicate Logic

Unnecessary Loops

Optimize:

Modules

Events

Memory Usage

Rendering

Execution Time

============================================================
8. RENDERING PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Reduce:

Layout Thrashing

Forced Reflows

Repaints

Heavy Animations

Keep rendering efficient.

============================================================
9. NETWORK PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Reduce:

HTTP Requests

Large Payloads

Duplicate Downloads

Unused Resources

Support:

Compression

Caching

HTTP/2+

CDN

============================================================
10. API PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Optimize:

Response Time

Pagination

Filtering

Caching

Serialization

Compression

Avoid over-fetching.

============================================================
11. DATABASE PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Monitor:

Slow Queries

Indexes

Execution Plans

Joins

Transactions

Storage Growth

Database performance directly affects user experience.

============================================================
12. CACHING STRATEGY
============================================================

Support:

Browser Cache

Memory Cache

CDN Cache

API Cache

Database Cache

Offline Cache (Future)

Cache only when it improves measurable performance.

============================================================
13. MEDIA DELIVERY
============================================================

Deliver:

Images

Videos

PDFs

Documents

using optimized delivery methods.

Large educational resources should load progressively.

============================================================
14. LAZY LOADING
============================================================

Apply lazy loading to:

Images

Videos

Long Lists

Course Thumbnails

Exercise Library

Anatomy Library

Load resources only when needed.

============================================================
15. CODE SPLITTING
============================================================

Load JavaScript in smaller modules.

Examples

Authentication

Dashboard

Lessons

Exercises

Community

AI

Users should not download unused code.

============================================================
16. MEMORY MANAGEMENT
============================================================

Avoid:

Memory Leaks

Unused Objects

Unreleased Resources

Infinite Listeners

Monitor memory usage continuously.

============================================================
17. ANIMATION PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Animations should:

Use GPU Acceleration where appropriate.

Remain smooth.

Avoid blocking rendering.

Prefer transform and opacity animations.

============================================================
18. MOBILE PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Optimize for:

Low-End Devices

Slow Networks

Battery Usage

Touch Responsiveness

Mobile users should receive the same educational experience.

============================================================
19. PERFORMANCE MONITORING
============================================================

Continuously monitor:

Page Load Time

API Latency

Database Performance

Rendering Time

Memory Usage

CPU Usage

Network Requests

Monitoring enables continuous optimization.

============================================================
20. PERFORMANCE BUDGET
============================================================

Every feature should have a performance budget.

Examples

Maximum Bundle Size

Maximum Image Size

Maximum API Response Time

Maximum Initial Load

Features exceeding budgets should be optimized before release.

============================================================
21. ACCESSIBILITY & PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Performance improvements should never reduce accessibility.

Both should improve together.

============================================================
22. AI PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Optimize:

Prompt Processing

Context Building

Response Time

Caching

Streaming Responses

AI should feel responsive.

============================================================
23. FUTURE PERFORMANCE STRATEGIES
============================================================

Future improvements may include:

Edge Computing

Server-Side Rendering

Static Generation

Predictive Prefetching

AI Optimization

Global CDN

Image CDN

Streaming Architecture

============================================================
24. PERFORMANCE TESTING
============================================================

Every release should include:

Load Testing

Stress Testing

Rendering Tests

API Benchmarks

Database Benchmarks

Mobile Benchmarks

Performance testing should be continuous.

============================================================
25. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Students should spend their time learning—

not waiting.

Every optimization,

no matter how small,

contributes to a faster,

more enjoyable,

and more effective educational experience.

Performance is part of the educational product.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 13

MANUAL 14

ACCESSIBILITY (WCAG) ENGINEERING HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Accessibility Engineering standards for Night Gym Academy.

Accessibility is not an optional feature.

It is a fundamental requirement that ensures every learner—regardless of ability, disability, device, language, or environment—can successfully use the platform.

Night Gym Academy should provide equal educational opportunities for everyone.

============================================================
1. ACCESSIBILITY PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Accessibility is education.

If a student cannot use the platform,

the educational mission has failed.

Accessibility should be integrated into every stage of development.

============================================================
2. ACCESSIBILITY STANDARD
============================================================

Night Gym Academy should follow:

WCAG 2.2

Target Compliance

Level AA

Future Goal

AAA where practical.

Accessibility should never be sacrificed for visual appearance.

============================================================
3. CORE PRINCIPLES
============================================================

Perceivable

Operable

Understandable

Robust

Every feature should satisfy these four principles.

============================================================
4. VISUAL ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Ensure:

High Color Contrast

Readable Fonts

Clear Typography

Scalable Text

Visible Focus

Responsive Layout

Visual clarity improves learning.

============================================================
5. KEYBOARD NAVIGATION
============================================================

Every feature must be usable without a mouse.

Support:

Tab Navigation

Shift + Tab

Arrow Keys

Escape

Enter

Space

No keyboard traps.

============================================================
6. SCREEN READER SUPPORT
============================================================

Support:

Semantic HTML

ARIA Labels

Headings

Lists

Buttons

Forms

Navigation

Dialogs

Screen readers should understand page structure.

============================================================
7. IMAGES
============================================================

Every educational image should include:

Alternative Text

Meaningful Description

Context

Decorative images should use empty alt attributes.

Images should teach everyone.

============================================================
8. VIDEO ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Educational videos should support:

Subtitles

Captions

Transcripts

Playback Controls

Volume Control

Pause

Replay

Students should learn regardless of hearing ability.

============================================================
9. AUDIO ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Audio resources should include:

Text Transcript

Playback Controls

Volume Control

Pause

Replay

Audio should never be the only way to deliver important information.

============================================================
10. FORMS
============================================================

Every form should include:

Labels

Instructions

Validation

Helpful Error Messages

Required Indicators

Keyboard Support

Forms should never confuse users.

============================================================
11. ERROR MESSAGES
============================================================

Errors should explain:

What happened.

Why it happened.

How to fix it.

Avoid vague messages.

============================================================
12. FOCUS MANAGEMENT
============================================================

Visible keyboard focus is mandatory.

Dialogs should trap focus appropriately.

Focus should return logically after dialogs close.

Users should always know where they are.

============================================================
13. COLOR USAGE
============================================================

Never communicate information using color alone.

Combine color with:

Icons

Text

Labels

Patterns

Everyone should understand the interface.

============================================================
14. RESPONSIVE ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Accessibility should remain effective across:

Desktop

Laptop

Tablet

Mobile

Portrait

Landscape

Accessibility should not break on smaller screens.

============================================================
15. LANGUAGE SUPPORT
============================================================

Support:

RTL

LTR

Language Attributes

Localized Labels

Localized Error Messages

Accessibility includes language.

============================================================
16. MOTION & ANIMATIONS
============================================================

Animations should:

Be subtle.

Avoid flashing.

Respect reduced motion preferences.

Never trigger discomfort.

Motion should improve—not hinder—the experience.

============================================================
17. EDUCATIONAL ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Educational content should provide:

Clear Headings

Short Paragraphs

Lists

Summaries

Key Points

Definitions

Revision Sections

Accessibility improves comprehension.

============================================================
18. TESTING
============================================================

Accessibility testing should include:

Keyboard Testing

Screen Reader Testing

Contrast Testing

Responsive Testing

Form Testing

Navigation Testing

Accessibility should be tested continuously.

============================================================
19. COMMON ACCESSIBILITY ISSUES
============================================================

Avoid:

Missing Labels

Poor Contrast

Tiny Buttons

Hidden Focus

Image-Only Buttons

Unlabeled Forms

Keyboard Traps

Unexpected Motion

Accessibility issues reduce educational quality.

============================================================
20. FUTURE ACCESSIBILITY FEATURES
============================================================

Future enhancements include:

Voice Navigation

Speech Recognition

Text-To-Speech

AI Accessibility Assistant

Reading Mode

High Contrast Mode

Custom Font Size

Simplified Interface

Adaptive Learning Support

============================================================
21. ACCESSIBILITY REVIEW CHECKLIST
============================================================

Before approval verify:

☐ Keyboard Navigation

☐ Screen Reader Support

☐ Proper Headings

☐ Accessible Forms

☐ Visible Focus

☐ Alternative Text

☐ Color Contrast

☐ Responsive Accessibility

☐ WCAG Compliance

============================================================
22. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Accessibility is not about compliance.

Accessibility is about inclusion.

Every student deserves the opportunity to learn,

regardless of physical ability,

device,

language,

or environment.

Night Gym Academy should be a platform where education is available to everyone.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 14

MANUAL 15

INTERNATIONALIZATION (i18n) & LOCALIZATION (l10n) HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Internationalization (i18n) and Localization (l10n) standards for Night Gym Academy.

The platform is designed from the beginning to become an international educational product.

Every feature should be developed so that adding a new language or entering a new country requires minimal engineering effort.

Internationalization should be built into the architecture—not added later.

============================================================
1. PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Night Gym Academy is not built for one country.

It is built for the world.

Every engineering decision should support international expansion.

============================================================
2. DEFINITIONS
============================================================

Internationalization (i18n)

Designing software so it supports multiple languages and regions.

Localization (l10n)

Adapting the software for a specific language, culture, and region.

Translation

Converting text between languages.

Localization goes beyond translation.

============================================================
3. SUPPORTED LANGUAGES
============================================================

Initial Languages

English

Arabic

Future Languages

French

German

Spanish

Portuguese

Italian

Turkish

Russian

Chinese

Japanese

Korean

Hindi

Urdu

Indonesian

Additional languages should be easy to add.

============================================================
4. TEXT MANAGEMENT
============================================================

Never hardcode user-facing text.

All interface text should come from translation files.

Examples

Buttons

Menus

Forms

Messages

Notifications

Errors

Dialogs

Lessons

Quizzes

Certificates

============================================================
5. TRANSLATION FILES
============================================================

Recommended Structure

translations/

en/

common.json

auth.json

courses.json

dashboard.json

errors.json

notifications.json

ai.json

ar/

common.json

auth.json

courses.json

dashboard.json

errors.json

notifications.json

ai.json

Organize translations by feature.

============================================================
6. TRANSLATION KEYS
============================================================

Examples

auth.login

auth.logout

dashboard.welcome

lesson.next

course.start

exercise.instructions

Avoid using full sentences as keys.

============================================================
7. RTL & LTR SUPPORT
============================================================

Support:

RTL

Arabic

Urdu

LTR

English

French

German

Spanish

The layout should automatically adapt.

============================================================
8. DATE & TIME
============================================================

Display:

Date

Time

Timezone

Calendar

according to user locale.

Never assume one date format.

============================================================
9. NUMBER FORMATTING
============================================================

Support localized formatting for:

Numbers

Percentages

Currency

Measurements

Scientific Values

Use locale-aware formatting.

============================================================
10. UNITS
============================================================

Support:

Metric

Imperial

Examples

kg / lb

cm / in

km / miles

Students should choose their preferred unit system.

============================================================
11. CURRENCY
============================================================

Future support:

USD

EUR

GBP

EGP

SAR

AED

JPY

INR

Currency formatting should follow regional standards.

============================================================
12. MEDIA LOCALIZATION
============================================================

Support localized:

Images

Videos

Voiceovers

Subtitles

PDF Files

Certificates

Media should match the user's language whenever possible.

============================================================
13. CULTURAL ADAPTATION
============================================================

Consider:

Images

Examples

Food

Exercises

Names

Symbols

Colors

Localization should respect cultural differences.

============================================================
14. SEARCH
============================================================

Search should support:

Multiple Languages

Synonyms

Localized Keywords

Scientific Names

Arabic

English

Future Languages

Users should find content regardless of language.

============================================================
15. AI LOCALIZATION
============================================================

AI should:

Respond in the user's language.

Understand localized terminology.

Recognize regional spelling.

Preserve scientific accuracy.

AI should feel native in every language.

============================================================
16. DATABASE SUPPORT
============================================================

Database should support:

Unicode

UTF-8

Localized Content

Multiple Languages

Translation Tables

Language Metadata

The database should never limit expansion.

============================================================
17. ACCESSIBILITY
============================================================

Localization should preserve accessibility.

Support:

Screen Readers

RTL

LTR

Localized Labels

Localized Errors

Accessibility should exist in every language.

============================================================
18. QUALITY ASSURANCE
============================================================

Before publishing a translation:

Scientific Review

Grammar Review

Native Review

Terminology Review

UI Review

RTL/LTR Testing

Translation quality affects educational quality.

============================================================
19. FUTURE FEATURES
============================================================

Future localization may include:

Automatic Translation Suggestions

AI Translation Assistant

Regional Course Catalogs

Country-Specific Certifications

Localized AI Models

Regional Pricing

Localized Community Spaces

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Language should never become a barrier to education.

Every student,

regardless of country,

culture,

or native language,

should receive the same high-quality educational experience.

Night Gym Academy should feel like a local platform—

everywhere in the world.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 15

MANUAL 16

ANALYTICS & DATA ENGINEERING HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Analytics and Data Engineering standards for Night Gym Academy.

Its purpose is to ensure that every important event inside the platform can be measured, analyzed, and transformed into meaningful insights.

Data should support better educational decisions—not simply generate reports.

Analytics should help improve learning, product quality, business growth, and user experience.

============================================================
1. DATA PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Collect only meaningful data.

Measure only what creates value.

Respect user privacy.

Transform data into decisions.

Every metric should answer an important question.

============================================================
2. ANALYTICS OBJECTIVES
============================================================

Analytics should answer:

How are students learning?

Where do students struggle?

Which lessons perform best?

Which exercises are most viewed?

How effective is AI?

How healthy is the business?

How can the platform improve?

============================================================
3. ANALYTICS CATEGORIES
============================================================

Educational Analytics

Student Analytics

Course Analytics

Exercise Analytics

Anatomy Analytics

Nutrition Analytics

Community Analytics

AI Analytics

Business Analytics

Infrastructure Analytics

============================================================

============================================================

Examples

Login

Logout

Course Started

Lesson Opened

Lesson Completed

Exercise Viewed

Exam Started

Exam Submitted

Certificate Generated

AI Chat Started

Search Performed

Payment Completed

Events create measurable behavior.

Timestamp

User ID

Device

Platform

8. EXERCISE ANALYTICS

9. AI ANALYTICS

============================================================
10. SEARCH ANALYTICS
============================================================

============================================================
11. BUSINESS ANALYTICS
============================================================

Track:

============================================================

============================================================

Each dashboard shows only relevant information.

============================================================
15. DATA STORAGE
============================================================

Analytics data should be:

Scalable

Data should support long-term analysis.

============================================================
16. REPORTING
============================================================

Generate reports:

Daily

============================================================

19. FUTURE ANALYTICS

============================================================

should ultimately improve education.

Night Gym Academy should become a data-informed educational platform—

never a data-driven platform that forgets its educational mission.

MANUAL 17

GIT, VERSION CONTROL & COLLABORATION HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Version Control and Collaboration standards for Night Gym Academy.

Its purpose is to ensure that every code change is traceable, reversible, reviewable, and understandable.

Version control protects the project from accidental data loss, conflicting changes, undocumented modifications, and poor collaboration.

Every contributor must follow these standards.

============================================================
1. VERSION CONTROL PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Every change matters.

Every change should be documented.

Every change should be reviewable.

Every change should be reversible.

Version history is part of the project's documentation.

============================================================
2. SOURCE OF TRUTH
============================================================

The Git repository is the official source of truth.

No code should exist outside version control.

Never deploy code that is not committed.

============================================================
3. BRANCHING STRATEGY
============================================================

Recommended Branches

main

Stable production code.

develop

Active development.

feature/*

New features.

bugfix/*

Bug fixes.

hotfix/*

Emergency production fixes.

release/*

Release preparation.

Every branch has one responsibility.

============================================================
4. BRANCH NAMING
============================================================

Examples

feature/authentication

feature/exercise-library

feature/anatomy-system

feature/ai-coach

feature/payment-system

bugfix/login-validation

bugfix/course-progress

hotfix/payment-error

release/v1.0.0

Branch names should clearly describe their purpose.

============================================================
5. COMMIT PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

A commit should represent one logical change.

Avoid mixing unrelated changes.

Small commits are easier to review.

============================================================
6. COMMIT MESSAGE STANDARD
============================================================

Use imperative verbs.

Examples

Add authentication middleware

Improve lesson navigation

Fix certificate generation

Update anatomy documentation

Refactor progress tracker

Avoid

update

fix

changes

done

test

============================================================
7. COMMIT STRUCTURE
============================================================

Recommended format

Title

Blank Line

Detailed Description

Reason

Breaking Changes (if any)

Issue Reference

Every important commit should explain why.

============================================================
8. PULL REQUESTS
============================================================

Every Pull Request should include:

Purpose

Summary

Files Changed

Testing Performed

Screenshots (UI Changes)

Documentation Updates

Known Limitations

PRs should remain focused.

============================================================
9. CODE REVIEW
============================================================

Review:

Architecture

Code Quality

Performance

Security

Accessibility

Documentation

Consistency

Educational Value

Review improves quality.

============================================================
10. MERGE STRATEGY
============================================================

Merge only after:

Code Review

Testing

Documentation

Approval

Conflict Resolution

Never merge unreviewed code.

============================================================
11. TAGGING
============================================================

Create Git Tags for:

Major Releases

Minor Releases

Patch Releases

Hotfixes

Examples

v1.0.0

v1.1.0

v1.1.3

============================================================
12. RELEASE BRANCHES
============================================================

Release branches allow:

Final Testing

Documentation Updates

Version Changes

Bug Fixes

without blocking future development.

============================================================
13. HOTFIX WORKFLOW
============================================================

Production

↓

Hotfix Branch

↓

Testing

↓

Review

↓

Production

↓

Merge Back

Hotfixes should remain isolated.

============================================================
14. CONFLICT RESOLUTION
============================================================

When merge conflicts occur:

Understand both changes.

Avoid deleting work.

Review architecture.

Test after resolving.

Document important resolutions.

============================================================
15. PROTECTED BRANCHES
============================================================

Protect:

main

release/*

Only approved contributors may merge.

============================================================
16. DOCUMENTATION CHANGES
============================================================

Whenever code changes:

Update Documentation.

Update Changelog.

Update Project State.

Documentation should never fall behind implementation.

============================================================
17. VERSIONING
============================================================

Follow Semantic Versioning.

Major

Breaking Changes

Minor

New Features

Patch

Bug Fixes

Version numbers communicate project maturity.

============================================================
18. BACKUP STRATEGY
============================================================

Protect the repository using:

Remote Repository

Mirrors

Tags

Releases

Backups

Version control is not a replacement for backups.

============================================================
19. FUTURE WORKFLOW
============================================================

Future improvements include:

GitHub Actions

Automated Releases

Automatic Changelog

CI/CD Integration

Code Owners

Protected Reviews

Issue Templates

Project Boards

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Every line of code tells part of the project's story.

Git preserves that story.

A clean commit history,

clear branches,

meaningful reviews,

and disciplined collaboration

allow Night Gym Academy to continue growing safely for many years.

Version control protects both the software—

and the people building it.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 17

============================================================
============================================================
MANUAL 18

CODE REVIEW & SOFTWARE QUALITY HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official Code Review process for Night Gym Academy.

Code Review is one of the most important quality assurance activities in the project.

Its purpose is not to criticize developers.

Its purpose is to improve software quality, maintain consistency, reduce bugs, preserve architecture, and help developers continuously improve.

Every code contribution should pass through this review process before becoming part of the project.

============================================================
1. CODE REVIEW PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Code Review exists to improve:

Quality

Maintainability

Security

Performance

Consistency

Knowledge Sharing

Architecture

Education

A successful review improves both the code and the developer.

============================================================
2. REVIEW OBJECTIVES
============================================================

Every review should answer:

Is the feature correct?

Is the implementation secure?

Is the code readable?

Is the architecture respected?

Is the documentation updated?

Can future developers understand this?

============================================================
3. REVIEW RESPONSIBILITIES
============================================================

Reviewer Responsibilities

Read carefully.

Understand the objective.

Provide constructive feedback.

Protect architecture.

Protect quality.

Protect maintainability.

Developer Responsibilities

Explain implementation.

Respond professionally.

Improve the code.

Update documentation.

Respect review decisions.

============================================================
4. REVIEW CHECKLIST
============================================================

Review:

Correctness

Architecture

Performance

Security

Accessibility

Documentation

Naming

Code Style

Maintainability

Scalability

Educational Value

No category should be skipped.

============================================================
5. ARCHITECTURE REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Project Structure

Folder Organization

Component Reuse

Service Separation

Database Impact

API Design

No architectural shortcuts.

============================================================
6. READABILITY REVIEW
============================================================

Code should be:

Simple

Clear

Self-Documenting

Well Named

Easy To Follow

Future developers should understand the code quickly.

============================================================
7. SECURITY REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Authentication

Authorization

Input Validation

Secrets

Permissions

Logging

Encryption

Security should never be assumed.

============================================================
8. PERFORMANCE REVIEW
============================================================

Review:

Queries

Loops

Rendering

Memory

Network Requests

Caching

Loading Speed

Performance problems should be solved before release.

============================================================
9. UI REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Style Lock

Spacing

Typography

Components

Animations

Responsiveness

Accessibility

Consistency

Every page should match the design system.

============================================================
10. BACKEND REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Business Logic

Validation

Error Handling

Logging

API Design

Database Access

Transactions

Background Jobs

Backend code should remain modular.

============================================================
11. DATABASE REVIEW
============================================================

Review:

Normalization

Indexes

Relationships

Constraints

Naming

Migration Safety

Rollback

Database changes require special attention.

============================================================
12. DOCUMENTATION REVIEW
============================================================

Verify updates to:

README

Project State

Architecture

API Documentation

Changelog

Developer Guide

Documentation should evolve with implementation.

============================================================
13. TESTING REVIEW
============================================================

Verify:

Unit Tests

Integration Tests

Regression Tests

Manual Testing

Accessibility

Performance

Security

Untested code should not be merged.

============================================================
14. EDUCATIONAL REVIEW
============================================================

When reviewing educational systems:

Scientific Accuracy

Terminology

Learning Objectives

References

Student Experience

Educational quality has the highest priority.

============================================================
15. COMMON REVIEW ISSUES
============================================================

Examples

Duplicate Code

Large Functions

Poor Naming

Hardcoded Values

Unused Code

Missing Validation

Weak Documentation

Missing Tests

Review should identify these early.

============================================================
16. REVIEW FEEDBACK
============================================================

Feedback should be:

Professional

Specific

Actionable

Respectful

Educational

Explain why—not only what.

============================================================
17. APPROVAL CRITERIA
============================================================

Approve only if:

Architecture Respected

Tests Passed

Documentation Updated

Security Verified

Performance Acceptable

Accessibility Verified

No Critical Issues

============================================================
18. WHEN TO REQUEST CHANGES
============================================================

Request changes if:

Architecture Broken

Security Risk

Poor Readability

Missing Tests

Missing Documentation

Performance Problems

Accessibility Issues

Constructive feedback improves the project.

============================================================
19. KNOWLEDGE SHARING
============================================================

Every review should help developers learn:

Better Architecture

Cleaner Code

Better Naming

Better Design

Better Security

Better Engineering

Code Review is also training.

============================================================
20. REVIEW METRICS
============================================================

Track:

Review Time

Approval Rate

Rework Rate

Review Comments

Critical Issues Found

Bugs Prevented

Review quality should improve over time.

============================================================
21. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The goal of Code Review is not to find mistakes.

The goal is to ensure that every contribution makes Night Gym Academy stronger than it was before.

Every review protects the future of the project.

Every approved change becomes part of the platform's legacy.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 18
