MANUAL 19

PROJECT ONBOARDING HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This manual defines the official onboarding process for every new contributor joining the Night Gym Academy project.

A contributor may be:

Software Engineer

UI/UX Designer

Backend Developer

Database Engineer

AI Assistant

Content Writer

Scientific Reviewer

QA Engineer

DevOps Engineer

Project Manager

Translator

Regardless of role, everyone should understand the project before making changes.

The objective is to reduce onboarding time while preserving quality and consistency.

============================================================
1. ONBOARDING PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Never begin contributing immediately.

Understand first.

Observe second.

Learn third.

Contribute fourth.

Understanding the project is part of the job.

============================================================
2. FIRST DAY CHECKLIST
============================================================

Every contributor should:

Understand the project vision.

Read the documentation.

Understand the architecture.

Understand the design system.

Understand the development workflow.

Understand project goals.

Meet the team (if applicable).

No contributor should begin development without completing onboarding.

============================================================
3. REQUIRED READING ORDER
============================================================

Read the following documents in order:

1. START_HERE.md

2. README.md

3. PROJECT_CONTEXT.md

4. PROJECT_STATE.md

5. STYLE_LOCK.md

6. AI_MASTER_PROMPT.md

7. PROJECT_PRINCIPLES.md

8. MASTER_DEVELOPMENT_CHECKLIST.md

9. Architecture Documentation

10. Relevant Manual for Your Role

Understanding the documentation comes before writing code.

============================================================
4. PROJECT UNDERSTANDING
============================================================

Every contributor should understand:

Project Mission

Educational Philosophy

Target Users

Business Goals

Architecture

Technology Stack

Future Vision

No work should begin without this understanding.

============================================================
5. ROLE-SPECIFIC ONBOARDING
============================================================

Frontend Engineers

Read:

Frontend Standards

UI Components

Style Lock

Accessibility

Backend Engineers

Read:

Backend Standards

API Standards

Database Guide

Security Handbook

Database Engineers

Read:

Database Engineering Guide

Architecture

Performance Handbook

AI Engineers

Read:

AI Engineering Guide

Knowledge Base

Prompt Standards

Content Writers

Read:

Content Writing Guide

Scientific Review Handbook

Translation Standards

Each role has specialized documentation.

============================================================
6. DEVELOPMENT ENVIRONMENT
============================================================

Every contributor should:

Clone Repository

Install Dependencies

Configure Environment

Verify Project Builds

Run Tests

Read Documentation

Verify Local Development

The local environment should match project standards.

============================================================
7. UNDERSTANDING THE CODEBASE
============================================================

Before modifying code:

Understand folder structure.

Understand reusable components.

Understand naming conventions.

Understand architecture.

Understand existing patterns.

Avoid introducing inconsistent code.

============================================================
8. UNDERSTANDING THE DESIGN
============================================================

Every contributor should understand:

Dark Theme

Component Library

Spacing System

Typography

Color System

Animations

Responsive Layout

Design consistency is mandatory.

============================================================
9. UNDERSTANDING THE EDUCATIONAL MODEL
============================================================

Every contributor should understand that Night Gym Academy is:

An educational platform.

Not a generic fitness website.

Education drives every decision.

============================================================
10. FIRST CONTRIBUTION
============================================================

Recommended first contribution:

Documentation

Minor Bug Fix

Small UI Improvement

Simple Refactoring

Small Feature

Avoid major architectural changes initially.

============================================================
11. COMMUNICATION
============================================================

Contributors should:

Ask questions.

Document assumptions.

Respect existing architecture.

Review documentation before proposing changes.

Good communication prevents mistakes.

============================================================
12. COMMON MISTAKES
============================================================

Avoid:

Skipping Documentation

Ignoring Style Lock

Duplicating Components

Changing Architecture

Hardcoding Values

Ignoring Accessibility

Ignoring Scientific Standards

Most mistakes come from insufficient understanding.

============================================================
13. SUCCESS CRITERIA
============================================================

A contributor is successfully onboarded when they can:

Explain the project.

Navigate the documentation.

Understand the architecture.

Follow coding standards.

Respect design rules.

Implement features consistently.

============================================================
14. CONTINUOUS LEARNING
============================================================

Contributors should regularly review:

Architecture Updates

Documentation Changes

New Standards

Release Notes

Manual Updates

The project evolves continuously.

============================================================
15. AI ONBOARDING
============================================================

Before generating any code, an AI assistant should:

Read START_HERE.md

Read PROJECT_STATE.md

Read STYLE_LOCK.md

Read AI_MASTER_PROMPT.md

Read the relevant engineering manual.

Understand the latest completed milestone.

Continue development without redesigning or rewriting completed work.

============================================================
16. MENTORING
============================================================

Experienced contributors should help new contributors understand:

Architecture

Standards

Best Practices

Documentation

Educational Philosophy

Knowledge sharing strengthens the team.

============================================================
17. ONBOARDING REVIEW
============================================================

Before full project access:

Verify documentation has been read.

Verify development environment.

Verify coding standards.

Verify architecture understanding.

Verify workflow understanding.

============================================================
18. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The fastest contributor is not the one who starts coding first.

The fastest contributor is the one who understands the project deeply before making the first change.

Understanding creates consistency.

Consistency creates quality.

Quality creates trust.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 19

============================================================
MANUAL 20

FOUNDER VISION & PROJECT PHILOSOPHY HANDBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This handbook preserves the original vision behind Night Gym Academy.

Technology changes.

Programming languages evolve.

Frameworks become obsolete.

Business models adapt.

But the vision behind the project should remain stable.

This document exists to ensure that every future developer, AI assistant, designer, manager, investor, or contributor understands not only what Night Gym Academy is—

but why it exists.

============================================================
1. THE VISION
============================================================

Night Gym Academy exists to become one of the world's leading educational platforms in fitness, anatomy, nutrition, biomechanics, coaching, and sports science.

The objective is not simply to teach workouts.

The objective is to educate people so they understand the science behind human performance.

============================================================
2. THE MISSION
============================================================

To make high-quality fitness education accessible to anyone, anywhere, regardless of language, financial background, or previous experience.

Education should not be limited by geography.

Knowledge should be available to everyone.

============================================================
3. THE LONG-TERM GOAL
============================================================

Night Gym Academy is intended to become:

A global educational institution.

A trusted scientific reference.

A professional certification platform.

A technology company.

An AI-powered learning ecosystem.

The goal extends far beyond creating a website.

============================================================
4. THE CORE BELIEF
============================================================

Knowledge changes lives.

A well-educated coach can improve hundreds of lives.

A well-educated student can improve their own life forever.

Education creates long-term impact.

============================================================
5. THE EDUCATIONAL PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Students should understand concepts—

not memorize facts.

Every lesson should answer:

Why?

How?

When?

What if?

Education should develop thinking,

not repetition.

============================================================
6. SCIENTIFIC RESPONSIBILITY
============================================================

Every educational statement should be:

Evidence-Based

Transparent

Current

Professionally Reviewed

Scientific integrity should never be sacrificed for popularity.

============================================================
7. SOFTWARE PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Software exists to support education.

Technology is a tool.

Education is the purpose.

Every technical decision should ultimately improve learning.

============================================================
8. DESIGN PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

The interface should disappear behind the learning experience.

Students should focus on:

Knowledge

Progress

Practice

Understanding

—not on figuring out how the application works.

============================================================
9. AI PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Artificial Intelligence should:

Teach.

Guide.

Explain.

Adapt.

Encourage.

Never replace human expertise.

Never replace scientific review.

Never replace critical thinking.

============================================================
10. QUALITY PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Quality is not something added before release.

Quality is part of every decision.

Every document.

Every lesson.

Every line of code.

Every animation.

Every database table.

Every API.

should reflect professional standards.

============================================================
11. BUSINESS PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Revenue supports education.

Education does not exist to maximize revenue.

Business success should make educational quality possible.

Never compromise educational integrity for short-term profit.

============================================================
12. PEOPLE FIRST
============================================================

Always prioritize:

Students

Instructors

Contributors

Developers

Community

Technology should serve people.

Never the opposite.

============================================================
13. GLOBAL THINKING
============================================================

Every feature should consider:

Languages

Cultures

Accessibility

International Expansion

Scalability

The platform should belong to the world.

============================================================
14. CONTINUOUS IMPROVEMENT
============================================================

Never assume the project is finished.

Continuously improve:

Educational Quality

Scientific Accuracy

Technology

Security

Accessibility

Performance

Documentation

Every release should move the platform forward.

============================================================
15. LEGACY
============================================================

Night Gym Academy should continue growing regardless of:

Technology Changes

Developer Changes

Leadership Changes

AI Evolution

Market Changes

The project should outlive the people who created it.

============================================================
16. THE ROLE OF CONTRIBUTORS
============================================================

Every contributor becomes a temporary guardian of the project.

Their responsibility is not merely to add features—

but to protect the platform's philosophy and quality.

============================================================
17. DECISION FRAMEWORK
============================================================

Before making any important decision, ask:

Does this improve education?

Does this improve quality?

Does this improve long-term maintainability?

Does this align with the project's vision?

If the answer is "No",

reconsider the decision.

============================================================
18. THE ROLE OF THE FOUNDER
============================================================

The Founder protects:

Vision

Educational Standards

Architecture

Brand Identity

Long-Term Strategy

Major Decisions

The Founder's responsibility is to ensure that the project never loses its purpose.

============================================================
19. THE ULTIMATE SUCCESS
============================================================

Success is not measured only by:

Revenue

Users

Downloads

Certificates

The greatest measure of success is the number of lives positively changed through education.

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Night Gym Academy is more than software.

It is more than an educational platform.

It is a long-term commitment to improving people's lives through knowledge.

Every lesson written,

every feature developed,

every bug fixed,

every design improved,

and every scientific review completed

should contribute to that mission.

Technology will evolve.

The vision should endure.

============================================================
END OF MANUAL 20

PLAYBOOK 01

ENTERPRISE OPERATIONS PLAYBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This playbook defines the operational procedures required to run Night Gym Academy as a professional software company.

While manuals explain engineering standards,

this playbook explains how the project operates every day.

It defines operational routines, responsibilities, communication, escalation paths, maintenance schedules, and decision-making processes.

Operations should remain predictable, measurable, and continuously improving.

============================================================
1. OPERATIONS PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Running a software platform requires more than writing code.

Daily operations include:

Monitoring

Support

Maintenance

Security

Content

Infrastructure

Business

Education

Operations keep the platform healthy.

============================================================
2. DAILY OPERATIONS
============================================================

Every day verify:

Platform Availability

Server Health

API Status

Database Status

AI Services

Error Logs

Security Events

Backups

Daily operations prevent small problems from becoming large problems.

============================================================
3. WEEKLY OPERATIONS
============================================================

Review:

Performance

Infrastructure

Documentation Updates

Weekly reviews maintain momentum.

============================================================
4. MONTHLY OPERATIONS
============================================================

Review:

Quarterly reviews guide strategic improvements.

============================================================

↓

↓

Assignment

↓

Investigation

↓

Mitigation

↓

Recovery

↓

Root Cause Analysis

↓

Documentation

↓

Process Improvement

Every incident becomes an opportunity to improve.

7. PRIORITY LEVELS
============================================================

Platform unavailable.

Priority 2

High

Major functionality affected.

Priority 3

Medium

Feature degradation.

Priority 4

Minor issues.

Operational response depends on priority.

============================================================

9. COMMUNICATION
============================================================

============================================================

Before operational changes:

============================================================

============================================================

============================================================

Operational excellence requires collaboration.

============================================================
15. FUTURE OPERATIONS
============================================================

Future operational capabilities may include:

Global Operations Center

============================================================
16. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Excellent operations are almost invisible.

Users simply experience a platform that is:

Reliable.

Secure.

Educational.

Operational excellence allows Night Gym Academy to focus on what matters most—

helping people learn.

# Purpose

This playbook defines how Night Gym Academy preserves knowledge, transfers responsibilities, and ensures that the project can continue growing regardless of changes in developers, AI assistants, managers, or leadership.

The project should never depend on one person.

Knowledge should become part of the project itself.

============================================================

============================================================

People change.

Technology changes.

Teams change.

Documentation remains.

The project should survive every transition.

2. KNOWLEDGE OWNERSHIP
============================================================

The Project

—not to individual contributors.

============================================================

Architecture

The project should remember everything—

even when people move on.

PLAYBOOK 03

DISASTER RECOVERY & BUSINESS CONTINUITY PLAYBOOK

============================================================
# Purpose
============================================================

This playbook defines the official Disaster Recovery (DR) and Business Continuity (BC) strategy for Night Gym Academy.

Unexpected failures are inevitable.

Professional organizations are defined not by the absence of failures—

but by how quickly and safely they recover.

The goal of this playbook is to minimize downtime, protect educational data, preserve user trust, and ensure uninterrupted learning.

============================================================
1. PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Every system should assume failure is possible.

Prepare before disaster.

Recover quickly.

Learn continuously.

Improve permanently.

Resilience is more valuable than perfection.

============================================================
2. CRITICAL ASSETS
============================================================

The following assets receive the highest protection priority:

User Accounts

Course Library

Lessons

Exercise Library

Anatomy Library

Nutrition Library

Certificates

Payments

Progress Tracking

Database

AI Knowledge

Source Code

Documentation

Infrastructure

============================================================
3. DISASTER CATEGORIES
============================================================

Infrastructure Failure

Database Failure

Cloud Provider Failure

Cyber Attack

Data Corruption

Human Error

Deployment Failure

Power Failure

Network Failure

Natural Disaster

Third-Party Service Failure

Multiple failures may occur simultaneously.

============================================================
4. RECOVERY PRIORITY
============================================================

Priority 1

Authentication

Priority 2

Database

Priority 3

Learning Platform

Priority 4

AI Services

Priority 5

Community

Priority 6

Analytics

Priority 7

Reporting

Restore educational functionality first.

============================================================
5. INCIDENT CLASSIFICATION
============================================================

Critical

Platform unavailable.

High

Major functionality unavailable.

Medium

Reduced functionality.

Low

Minor degradation.

Every incident receives a severity level.

============================================================
6. RECOVERY WORKFLOW
============================================================

Incident Detected

↓

Incident Confirmed

↓

Severity Assigned

↓

Response Team Activated

↓

Containment

↓

Recovery

↓

Validation

↓

Monitoring

↓

Documentation

↓

Lessons Learned

Recovery should follow one predictable process.

============================================================
7. DATABASE RECOVERY
============================================================

Recovery includes:

Backup Validation

Restore Latest Backup

Verify Integrity

Replay Transactions (If Available)

Application Verification

Production Approval

Database recovery should always be tested.

============================================================
8. INFRASTRUCTURE RECOVERY
============================================================

Restore:

Servers

Containers

Networking

Load Balancers

Storage

Monitoring

Infrastructure should be reproducible.

============================================================
9. APPLICATION RECOVERY
============================================================

Recover:

Backend

Frontend

APIs

Authentication

Background Jobs

AI Services

Every service should have a recovery procedure.

============================================================
10. BACKUP STRATEGY
============================================================

Support:

Real-Time Replication

Daily Incremental Backup

Weekly Full Backup

Monthly Archive

Offsite Backup

Encrypted Backup

Recovery Verification

Backups should never remain untested.

============================================================
11. COMMUNICATION
============================================================

During incidents communicate:

Current Status

Affected Services

Estimated Recovery

Progress Updates

Resolution

Post-Incident Report

Transparent communication builds trust.

============================================================
12. ROLLBACK
============================================================

Every deployment must support:

Immediate Rollback

Previous Version

Database Rollback

Configuration Rollback

Rollback should remain simple.

============================================================
13. BUSINESS CONTINUITY
============================================================

Educational continuity has highest priority.

Students should retain access whenever possible.

Critical educational services should remain operational even during partial outages.

============================================================
14. RESPONSIBILITIES
============================================================

Founder

Strategic Decisions

Engineering

Recovery

DevOps

Infrastructure

Database Engineer

Data Recovery

Security

Incident Investigation

QA

Verification

Support

User Communication

Everyone has a defined role.

============================================================
15. POST-INCIDENT REVIEW
============================================================

Every incident should document:

Timeline

Root Cause

Impact

Recovery Time

Lessons Learned

Preventive Actions

No incident should be forgotten.

============================================================
16. DISASTER TESTING
============================================================

Regularly simulate:

Server Failure

Database Failure

Backup Recovery

Deployment Failure

Network Failure

Recovery plans should be practiced.

============================================================
17. FUTURE IMPROVEMENTS
============================================================

Future capabilities include:

Multi-Region Deployment

Automatic Failover

Self-Healing Infrastructure

AI Incident Detection

Predictive Failure Analysis

Zero-Downtime Deployments

Disaster preparedness should evolve continuously.

============================================================
18. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

The true measure of a professional platform is not whether failures occur.

The true measure is how quickly,

how safely,

and how confidently

the platform recovers.

Night Gym Academy should always protect:

Knowledge.

Students.

Trust.

Continuity.

============================================================
END OF PLAYBOOK 03

PLAYBOOK 04

RELEASE OPERATIONS & DEPLOYMENT PLAYBOOK

============================================================

# Purpose

This playbook defines the official operational process for deploying new versions of Night Gym Academy.

Its objective is to ensure that every deployment is predictable, repeatable, secure, documented, and recoverable.

Deployments should never rely on luck.

Every release should follow the same disciplined workflow.

============================================================
1. DEPLOYMENT PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Deployment is not simply uploading code.

Deployment is the controlled transition from one stable version to another.

Every deployment should reduce risk—not introduce it.

============================================================
2. RELEASE TYPES
============================================================

Major Release

New platform capabilities.

Minor Release

New features and improvements.

Patch Release

Bug fixes.

Hotfix

Emergency production fix.

Every deployment belongs to one release type.

============================================================
3. PRE-DEPLOYMENT CHECKLIST
============================================================

Before deployment verify:

☐ Code Review Complete

☐ QA Approved

☐ Security Review Passed

☐ Documentation Updated

☐ Version Updated

☐ Database Migration Reviewed

☐ Rollback Plan Ready

☐ Backups Verified

☐ Monitoring Enabled

Deployment begins only after every checkpoint passes.

============================================================
4. DEPLOYMENT WORKFLOW
============================================================

Development

↓

Testing

↓

QA Approval

↓

Security Review

↓

Release Candidate

↓

Production Approval

↓

Deployment

↓

Monitoring

↓

Validation

↓

Release Confirmation

Every deployment follows this workflow.

============================================================
5. DATABASE DEPLOYMENT
============================================================

Database deployment includes:

Migration Scripts

Rollback Scripts

Data Validation

Backup

Integrity Verification

Migration Monitoring

Database deployment requires additional caution.

============================================================
6. CONFIGURATION DEPLOYMENT
============================================================

Verify:

Environment Variables

Secrets

API Keys

Cloud Configuration

Storage

Email

AI Providers

Configuration errors should be detected before deployment.

============================================================
7. INFRASTRUCTURE VALIDATION
============================================================

Verify:

Servers

Containers

Networking

Storage

CDN

DNS

Certificates

Monitoring

Infrastructure should be healthy before deployment.

============================================================
8. DEPLOYMENT APPROVAL
============================================================

Production deployment requires approval from:

Lead Developer

↓

QA

↓

DevOps

↓

Founder (Major Releases)

No unauthorized deployments.

============================================================
9. DEPLOYMENT MONITORING
============================================================

Immediately monitor:

Errors

CPU

Memory

Database

API

Authentication

Payments

AI

Traffic

Early detection minimizes impact.

============================================================
10. POST-DEPLOYMENT VALIDATION
============================================================

Verify:

Login

Registration

Courses

Lessons

Certificates

Payments

Community

AI

Notifications

Critical user journeys should always be tested.

============================================================
11. ROLLBACK CONDITIONS
============================================================

Rollback immediately if:

Critical Errors

Database Corruption

Authentication Failure

Payment Failure

Security Risk

Platform Instability

Rollback decisions should prioritize users.

============================================================
12. HOTFIX DEPLOYMENT
============================================================

Emergency workflow:

Problem

↓

Hotfix Branch

↓

Testing

↓

Approval

↓

Deployment

↓

Validation

↓

Merge Back

Hotfixes should remain isolated.

============================================================
13. RELEASE DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

Update:

Release Notes

CHANGELOG

PROJECT_STATE

Documentation

Architecture Records

Version History

Documentation completes the release.

============================================================
14. COMMUNICATION
============================================================

Notify stakeholders:

Deployment Start

Deployment Complete

Known Issues

Maintenance Windows

Rollback (If Needed)

Clear communication reduces uncertainty.

============================================================
15. MAINTENANCE WINDOWS
============================================================

Whenever possible:

Deploy during low traffic.

Announce maintenance.

Minimize downtime.

Prepare rollback.

Protect user progress.

============================================================
16. RELEASE METRICS
============================================================

Measure:

Deployment Duration

Deployment Success Rate

Rollback Rate

Incident Count

Recovery Time

Release Stability

# Purpose

Night Gym Academy is not only an educational platform.

# Purpose

This document defines the permanent operational rules that every Artificial Intelligence system must follow while contributing to the Night Gym Academy project.

These rules override personal preferences, default AI behavior, and generic software recommendations.

The AI should always behave as a professional member of the engineering team.

============================================================

============================================================

Always protect the project.

Before optimizing anything, understand it.

Before changing anything, document it.

Before replacing anything, justify it.

============================================================

============================================================

Never redesign the UI.

Never rename folders unnecessarily.

Never rewrite completed modules.

Never delete features without approval.

Never simplify enterprise architecture.

Never replace professional solutions with beginner solutions.

Never ignore existing documentation.

============================================================
3. ALWAYS DO THESE THINGS
============================================================

Read documentation first.

Understand context.

Continue existing work.

Preserve consistency.

Document major changes.

Respect the architecture.

# Purpose

This document defines what an AI system should remember during development while working on Night Gym Academy.

Unlike human memory, AI context is temporary.

This document provides a structured memory model that allows different AI systems to work consistently without losing project continuity.

AI memory should always be based on documentation—not assumptions.

============================================================

============================================================

The AI should never depend on memory alone.

Documentation is the permanent memory.

AI memory is only a temporary working context.

Whenever uncertainty exists,

documentation always overrides memory.

Project Name

Founder

Company

Architecture

============================================================

Never replace missing information with assumptions.

============================================================

============================================================

↓

============================================================

Users should never notice changes between AI models.

Consistency is more important than style.

============================================================
15. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Memory exists to preserve continuity.

Documentation exists to preserve truth.

Whenever the two disagree,

documentation always wins.

The AI should remember enough to work efficiently—

but always verify enough to work correctly.

# Purpose

This document defines the official task execution system for every Artificial Intelligence model working on the Night Gym Academy project.

Its purpose is to ensure that every task is completed using the same engineering workflow, regardless of which AI model performs the work.

AI should never jump directly into implementation.

A task is:

↓

↓

↓

Implement

↓

↓

↓

Complete

Backend

Database

API

AI

Infrastructure

Security

Documentation

Business

Content

Testing

Step 7

Validate.

↓

Reusable

Scalable

Secure

Maintainable

Readable

Avoid shortcuts.

============================================================
8. SELF REVIEW
============================================================

After implementation review:

Architecture

Naming

Performance

Accessibility

Security

Documentation

Code Quality

Review your own work before presenting it.

============================================================
9. VALIDATION
============================================================

Verify:

Requirements Met

No Broken Features

No Design Violations

No Documentation Gaps

No Security Risks

No Performance Regression

Validation completes development.

============================================================
10. DOCUMENTATION UPDATE
============================================================

Whenever implementation changes:

Update Documentation

Update Project State

Update Architecture Records (if necessary)

Update Changelog

Documentation is never optional.

============================================================
11. COMMUNICATION
============================================================

Responses should clearly explain:

Objective

Approach

Reasoning

Trade-offs

Next Steps

Communication should help future contributors.

============================================================
12. HANDLING MISSING CONTEXT
============================================================

If information is missing:

Pause implementation.

Identify missing documentation.

Request clarification.

Never invent architecture or business rules.

============================================================
13. CONTINUOUS CONSISTENCY
============================================================

Every response should preserve:

Architecture

UI Standards

Coding Standards

Educational Philosophy

Scientific Accuracy

Business Vision

Consistency is more important than creativity.

============================================================
14. FINAL VERIFICATION
============================================================

Before considering work complete verify:

☐ Objective Achieved

☐ Architecture Preserved

☐ Documentation Updated

☐ Style Lock Maintained

☐ Performance Acceptable

☐ Security Preserved

☐ Educational Value Improved

============================================================
15. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Every workflow exists for one reason:

To ensure that Night Gym Academy grows in a predictable,

professional,

maintainable,

and scalable way.

AI should never optimize for speed alone.

It should optimize for long-term excellence.

============================================================
END OF AI_WORKFLOW.md

============================================================
============================================================
AI CONTEXT 08

AI_CODE_RULES.md

============================================================

# Purpose

This document defines the official coding rules that every Artificial Intelligence system must follow when generating, modifying, or reviewing source code for Night Gym Academy.

These rules exist to guarantee that all generated code remains consistent, maintainable, scalable, secure, and production-ready.

AI should generate code that looks as though it was written by the same senior engineering team.

============================================================
1. CODING PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Write code for humans first.

Computers execute code.

Humans maintain it.

Readable code is professional code.

============================================================
2. GENERAL RULES
============================================================

Every generated code should be:

Readable

Modular

Reusable

Scalable

Documented

Consistent

Production Ready

Temporary solutions should be avoided.

============================================================
3. FILE ORGANIZATION
============================================================

Respect existing project structure.

Never:

Create random folders.

Duplicate existing modules.

Break architecture.

Move files unnecessarily.

Organization should remain predictable.

============================================================
4. NAMING CONVENTIONS
============================================================

Use descriptive names.

Examples

ExerciseCard

NutritionCalculator

UserProgressService

CertificateGenerator

Avoid names like:

temp

test1

newCode

data2

Names should explain purpose.

============================================================
5. FUNCTION RULES
============================================================

Functions should:

Have one responsibility.

Be easy to understand.

Avoid excessive length.

Return predictable results.

Minimize side effects.

Single Responsibility improves maintainability.

============================================================
6. COMPONENT RULES
============================================================

UI Components should be:

Reusable

Independent

Accessible

Responsive

Documented

Avoid duplicate components.

============================================================
7. COMMENTS
============================================================

Comments should explain:

Why

—not—

What

Use comments only when necessary.

Good code should explain itself.

============================================================
8. ERROR HANDLING
============================================================

Every critical operation should:

Handle failures.

Return meaningful errors.

Avoid exposing internal details.

Log unexpected failures.

Error handling is part of functionality.

============================================================
9. SECURITY
============================================================

Never:

Hardcode secrets.

Expose credentials.

Trust client input.

Ignore validation.

Bypass authentication.

Security should exist by default.

============================================================
10. PERFORMANCE
============================================================

Avoid:

Duplicate Logic

Unnecessary Rendering

Repeated Queries

Memory Leaks

Blocking Operations

Optimize only when measurable.

============================================================
11. DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

Whenever creating:

API

Component

Service

Module

Utility

Update related documentation.

Implementation and documentation should evolve together.

============================================================
12. DEPENDENCIES
============================================================

Before introducing a dependency ask:

Is it necessary?

Can existing tools solve the problem?

Is it actively maintained?

Does it increase complexity?

Avoid dependency bloat.

============================================================
13. TESTABILITY
============================================================

Generated code should be easy to test.

Separate:

Logic

UI

Database

Network

Configuration

Testable architecture improves reliability.

============================================================
14. BACKWARD COMPATIBILITY
============================================================

Avoid breaking:

Existing APIs

Existing Components

Existing Database

Existing User Flows

Breaking changes require explicit approval.

============================================================
15. STYLE CONSISTENCY
============================================================

Generated code should match:

Existing Formatting

Naming

Architecture

Folder Structure

Coding Standards

Consistency is more important than personal preference.

============================================================
16. CODE REVIEW READINESS
============================================================

Before presenting code verify:

Readability

Maintainability

Performance

Security

Documentation

Scalability

The code should be ready for review.

============================================================
17. FUTURE PROOFING
============================================================

Implement solutions that support:

Future Features

Future Scaling

Future AI

Future Localization

Future Documentation

Think beyond the current task.

============================================================
18. WHEN NOT TO WRITE CODE
============================================================

Do not generate code if:

Requirements are unclear.

Architecture is missing.

Business rules are incomplete.

Critical documentation is unavailable.

Ask for clarification first.

============================================================
19. PROFESSIONAL STANDARD
============================================================

Every generated file should appear suitable for:

Enterprise Production

Long-Term Maintenance

Team Collaboration

Future Expansion

Professional software lasts for years.

============================================================
20. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

AI should never generate code merely because it works.

AI should generate code that future engineers will enjoy maintaining.

Every file should improve the overall quality of Night Gym Academy.

============================================================
END OF AI_CODE_RULES.md

============================================================
============================================================
AI CONTEXT 09

AI_STYLE_RULES.md

============================================================

# Purpose

This document defines the official response style, communication standards, explanation methodology, and engineering communication rules for every Artificial Intelligence model working on Night Gym Academy.

Regardless of which AI model is used, responses should appear as though they were written by the same senior engineering team.

Consistency in communication is as important as consistency in code.

============================================================
1. COMMUNICATION PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Communication should always be:

Professional

Clear

Direct

Educational

Respectful

Constructive

Consistent

Every response should reduce confusion.

============================================================
2. RESPONSE OBJECTIVE
============================================================

The objective is not simply to answer questions.

The objective is to:

Educate

Guide

Explain

Recommend

Protect Architecture

Protect Quality

Improve Understanding

============================================================
3. WRITING STYLE
============================================================

Responses should be:

Well Structured

Easy To Read

Logically Organized

Technically Accurate

Free From Ambiguity

Avoid unnecessary verbosity.

Avoid unnecessary repetition.

============================================================
4. ENGINEERING TONE
============================================================

Always communicate like:

Senior Software Architect

Senior Engineer

Technical Consultant

Product Architect

Never communicate casually when discussing engineering decisions.

============================================================
5. EXPLANATION STYLE
============================================================

Whenever explaining technical concepts:

Start with the objective.

↓

Explain the reasoning.

↓

Describe the implementation.

↓

Mention trade-offs.

↓

Explain future impact.

Help users understand both "how" and "why."

============================================================
6. CODE PRESENTATION
============================================================

When presenting code:

Explain purpose first.

Then provide implementation.

Then explain important decisions.

Never present large code blocks without context.

============================================================
7. DESIGN DISCUSSIONS
============================================================

When discussing UI or UX:

Explain:

User Benefit

Consistency

Accessibility

Performance

Maintainability

Design decisions should always have justification.

============================================================
8. ARCHITECTURE DISCUSSIONS
============================================================

Whenever architecture is involved:

Identify affected systems.

Explain dependencies.

Explain scalability.

Protect modularity.

Avoid unnecessary redesign.

============================================================
9. DECISION EXPLANATIONS
============================================================

Every recommendation should answer:

Why this solution?

Why not alternatives?

How does it fit the architecture?

What are future implications?

Engineering decisions should always be justified.

============================================================
10. HANDLING DISAGREEMENT
============================================================

If a proposed solution conflicts with project standards:

Explain the conflict.

Reference project philosophy.

Recommend an alternative.

Protect long-term quality.

Professional disagreement improves the project.

============================================================
11. EDUCATIONAL STYLE
============================================================

When explaining educational content:

Be scientifically accurate.

Avoid unnecessary jargon.

Use examples.

Use step-by-step reasoning.

Encourage understanding—not memorization.

============================================================
12. HANDLING UNCERTAINTY
============================================================

If uncertain:

State uncertainty.

Explain missing information.

Request clarification.

Avoid assumptions.

Professional honesty builds trust.

============================================================
13. DOCUMENTATION STYLE
============================================================

Documentation should be:

Structured

Versioned

Consistent

Easy To Navigate

Future Friendly

Documentation should outlive implementation.

============================================================
14. CONSISTENCY
============================================================

Every response should remain consistent with:

Architecture

Design

Business Rules

Educational Philosophy

Engineering Standards

Never contradict established documentation.

============================================================
15. RESPONSE QUALITY CHECK
============================================================

Before responding verify:

Accuracy

Clarity

Consistency

Professionalism

Educational Value

Architectural Alignment

Every response should pass this review.

============================================================
16. MULTI-AI CONSISTENCY
============================================================

Different AI models should produce responses that feel like they came from one engineering organization.

The project's communication style should remain independent of the model being used.

============================================================
17. FUTURE COMMUNICATION
============================================================

Future AI systems should support:

Voice

Video

Interactive Explanations

Visual Diagrams

Collaborative Planning

Live Pair Programming

The communication philosophy should remain unchanged.

============================================================
18. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Good AI communication does more than answer questions.

It teaches.

It explains.

It protects quality.

It preserves consistency.

Every response should strengthen both the project and the people building it.

============================================================
END OF AI_STYLE_RULES.md

============================================================
============================================================
AI CONTEXT 10

AI_CONTINUATION.md

============================================================

# Purpose

This document defines how any Artificial Intelligence system should continue development after interruptions, context loss, model switching, or long periods of inactivity.

Large software projects are never completed in a single session.

This document ensures that development continues seamlessly regardless of which AI model resumes the project.

============================================================
1. CONTINUATION PHILOSOPHY
============================================================

Never restart the project.

Never redesign completed systems.

Never ignore previous work.

Continue from the latest verified project state.

Continuity is more important than speed.

============================================================
2. WHEN TO USE THIS DOCUMENT
============================================================

Use this document whenever:

A new AI model joins the project.

A conversation is restarted.

Context is lost.

Development resumes after a long break.

A different engineering team continues development.

This document restores continuity.

============================================================
3. FIRST ACTIONS
============================================================

Before generating any response:

Read

START_HERE.md

↓

PROJECT_CONTEXT.md

↓

PROJECT_STATE.md

↓

AI_PROJECT_STATE.md

↓

Relevant Manual

↓

Relevant Playbook

↓

Current Task

Never skip project recovery.

============================================================
4. PROJECT RECOVERY
============================================================

Recover:

Current Milestone

Completed Features

Architecture

Design System

Database Structure

Documentation Status

Pending Tasks

Project recovery should take priority over implementation.

============================================================
5. VERIFY PROJECT STATE
============================================================

Before coding verify:

Current Version

Latest Documentation

Recent Decisions

Known Issues

Roadmap Position

Architecture Lock

Implementation should always reflect reality.

============================================================
6. CONTINUE — DO NOT RESTART
============================================================

Always continue existing systems.

Never replace completed modules simply because another solution exists.

Respect engineering history.

Respect previous contributors.

Respect project evolution.

============================================================
7. PRESERVE CONSISTENCY
============================================================

Continue using:

Existing Components

Existing Folder Structure

Existing Naming

Existing Design

Existing Documentation

Consistency creates maintainability.

============================================================
8. CONTEXT RECOVERY CHECKLIST
============================================================

Before implementation verify:

☐ Current Milestone

☐ Relevant Documentation

☐ Style Lock

☐ Architecture

☐ Dependencies

☐ Existing Components

☐ Current Priorities

Recovery should be systematic.

============================================================
9. DECISION VALIDATION
============================================================

Whenever proposing a change ask:

Does this preserve architecture?

Does this preserve educational quality?

Does this preserve design consistency?

Does this preserve documentation quality?

Changes should strengthen—not reset—the project.

============================================================
10. DOCUMENT SYNCHRONIZATION
============================================================

Whenever development continues:

Verify:

Documentation

Architecture

Project State

AI Context

Roadmap

Synchronize before implementing.

============================================================
11. HANDLING OUTDATED CONTEXT
============================================================

If previous information conflicts with current documentation:

Trust the documentation.

Discard outdated assumptions.

Never preserve obsolete information.

Documentation is authoritative.

============================================================
12. MULTI-AI COLLABORATION
============================================================

Assume that multiple AI systems may contribute.

Every AI should:

Leave clear documentation.

Avoid hidden assumptions.

Respect previous work.

Prepare the project for the next contributor.

Engineering should be collaborative.

============================================================
13. SESSION COMPLETION
============================================================

Before ending any working session:

Document completed work.

Document pending work.

Update project state.

Update documentation if required.

Leave clear next steps.

Every session should prepare the next session.

============================================================
14. PROJECT MATURITY
============================================================

As Night Gym Academy grows:

Architecture becomes more stable.

Documentation becomes more important.

Consistency becomes more valuable.

Future contributors should change less—

and understand more.

============================================================
15. FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

Artificial Intelligence should never behave as though every conversation begins a new project.

Every conversation is simply another chapter in the same long-term engineering journey.

Continue the vision.

Protect the architecture.

Respect the documentation.

Improve the platform.

Leave the project better than you found it.

============================================================
END OF AI_CONTINUATION.md

============================================================

============================================================
MASTER GLOSSARY

Night Gym Academy Official Terminology

============================================================

Version

1.0.0

Status

Official

Purpose

This glossary defines the official terminology used throughout the Night Gym Academy project.

Its purpose is to ensure that developers, designers, AI systems, educators, researchers, business stakeholders, and future contributors all use the same language.

Consistent terminology improves communication, documentation, implementation, and long-term maintainability.

============================================================
A
============================================================

API

Application Programming Interface.

The communication layer between software systems.

------------------------------------------------------------

Architecture

The high-level structure of the software, including modules, layers, services, and their relationships.

------------------------------------------------------------

AI

Artificial Intelligence systems integrated into Night Gym Academy.

============================================================
B
============================================================

Backend

The server-side application responsible for business logic, APIs, authentication, and data processing.

------------------------------------------------------------

Bug

An unintended defect causing incorrect behavior.

------------------------------------------------------------

Business Rule

A rule that defines how the platform behaves from a business perspective.

============================================================
C
============================================================

Certificate

A digital credential awarded after successful completion of learning requirements.

------------------------------------------------------------

Component

A reusable UI building block.

------------------------------------------------------------

Context

Information required by AI or developers to correctly understand the current project state.

============================================================
D
============================================================

Database

Persistent storage for all application data.

------------------------------------------------------------

Dependency

A resource required by another component, module, or service.

------------------------------------------------------------

Deployment

The process of publishing a new software version.

============================================================
E
============================================================

Endpoint

A specific API URL providing access to functionality.

------------------------------------------------------------

Evidence-Based

Educational content supported by reliable scientific research.

============================================================
F
============================================================

Feature

A complete functional capability provided by the platform.

------------------------------------------------------------

Frontend

The user interface presented to learners.

============================================================
G
============================================================

Git

Version control system used to manage source code.

------------------------------------------------------------

Governance

Processes that ensure quality, consistency, and responsible decision-making.

============================================================
H
============================================================

Hotfix

An emergency software update released to fix a critical production issue.

============================================================
I
============================================================

Infrastructure

Servers, cloud services, networking, storage, and deployment environments.

------------------------------------------------------------

Integration Test

A test verifying interaction between multiple software components.

============================================================
J
============================================================

JSON

JavaScript Object Notation.

The standard data exchange format used throughout the project.

============================================================
K
============================================================

Knowledge Base

The structured collection of educational and technical information used by the platform and AI systems.

============================================================
L
============================================================

Lesson

The smallest structured educational unit delivered to students.

------------------------------------------------------------

Localization

Adapting content for a specific language or region.

============================================================
M
============================================================

Manual

A formal engineering document defining standards.

------------------------------------------------------------

Migration

A controlled database schema modification.

============================================================
N
============================================================

Night Gym Academy

The official name of the educational platform.

============================================================
O
============================================================

OpenAPI

The documentation standard used for REST APIs.

============================================================
P
============================================================

Playbook

A document describing operational procedures and workflows.

------------------------------------------------------------

Production

The live environment used by students.

============================================================
Q
============================================================

Quality Assurance (QA)

The process of verifying that software meets project standards.

============================================================
R
============================================================

Repository

The official Git source code repository.

------------------------------------------------------------

Rollback

Returning to a previous stable version after deployment issues.

============================================================
S
============================================================

Scientific Review

Professional verification of educational accuracy.

------------------------------------------------------------

Service

A backend module responsible for one business capability.

------------------------------------------------------------

Style Lock

The official visual design rules that should not be changed without approval.

============================================================
T
============================================================

Task

A defined unit of work with a clear objective.

------------------------------------------------------------

Technical Debt

Engineering compromises requiring future improvement.

============================================================
U
============================================================

UI

User Interface.

------------------------------------------------------------

UX

User Experience.

============================================================
V
============================================================

Version

A uniquely identified project release.

============================================================
W
============================================================

Workflow

A repeatable sequence of steps used to complete a process.

============================================================
Y
============================================================

YFLB

The parent company responsible for developing and operating Night Gym Academy.

============================================================
FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

A shared vocabulary creates shared understanding.

Every contributor—

developer,

designer,

researcher,

writer,

manager,

or AI system—

should use these definitions consistently.

Clear terminology reduces misunderstandings,

improves documentation,

and strengthens collaboration.

============================================================
END OF MASTER GLOSSARY

============================================================
============================================================
PROJECT_TREE

Night Gym Academy Project Structure

============================================================

Version

1.0.0

Status

Official

Purpose

This document defines the official directory structure of the Night Gym Academy project.

Its purpose is to provide every developer, AI system, and contributor with a complete map of the project.

The project structure should remain predictable, scalable, modular, and easy to navigate.

Folder organization is part of the software architecture.

============================================================
ROOT STRUCTURE
============================================================

```text
NightGymAcademy/

│

├── docs/

├── src/

├── public/

├── assets/

├── tests/

├── scripts/

├── database/

├── infrastructure/

├── api/

├── ai/

├── tools/

├── config/

├── .github/

├── package.json

├── README.md

└── LICENSE
```

============================================================
DOCUMENTATION
============================================================

```text
docs/

│

├── START_HERE.md

├── README.md

├── PROJECT_CONTEXT.md

├── PROJECT_STATE.md

├── STYLE_LOCK.md

├── MASTER_DOCUMENTATION.md

├── manuals/

├── playbooks/

├── ai/

├── architecture/

├── business/

├── changelog/

└── references/
```

Documentation should remain separated from source code.

============================================================
SOURCE CODE
============================================================

```text
src/

│

├── app/

├── components/

├── layouts/

├── pages/

├── routes/

├── services/

├── api/

├── hooks/

├── contexts/

├── stores/

├── utils/

├── constants/

├── types/

├── styles/

├── assets/

└── main
```

Every folder should have one clear responsibility.

============================================================
COMPONENTS
============================================================

```text
components/

│

├── common/

├── ui/

├── forms/

├── cards/

├── navigation/

├── charts/

├── ai/

├── education/

├── anatomy/

├── nutrition/

├── calculators/

└── community/
```

Components should remain reusable.

============================================================
PAGES
============================================================

```text
pages/

│

├── Home/

├── Dashboard/

├── Courses/

├── Lessons/

├── Anatomy/

├── Nutrition/

├── Exercises/

├── Calculators/

├── Community/

├── AI/

├── Profile/

├── Settings/

├── Authentication/

└── Admin/
```

Pages represent complete user experiences.

============================================================
BACKEND
============================================================

```text
api/

│

├── controllers/

├── services/

├── middleware/

├── routes/

├── validators/

├── repositories/

├── models/

├── jobs/

├── events/

├── policies/

└── utils/
```

Backend should remain layered.

============================================================
DATABASE
============================================================

```text
database/

│

├── schema/

├── migrations/

├── seeds/

├── backups/

├── scripts/

└── documentation/
```

Database changes should always use migrations.

============================================================
AI SYSTEM
============================================================

```text
ai/

│

├── prompts/

├── knowledge/

├── context/

├── workflows/

├── evaluation/

├── models/

├── safety/

├── analytics/

└── documentation/
```

AI should remain modular.

============================================================
TESTING
============================================================

```text
tests/

│

├── unit/

├── integration/

├── api/

├── e2e/

├── performance/

├── security/

├── accessibility/

└── fixtures/
```

Testing mirrors the project architecture.

============================================================
PUBLIC FILES
============================================================

```text
public/

│

├── images/

├── icons/

├── videos/

├── documents/

├── certificates/

└── manifest/
```

Only publicly accessible assets belong here.

============================================================
INFRASTRUCTURE
============================================================

```text
infrastructure/

│

├── docker/

├── kubernetes/

├── monitoring/

├── deployment/

├── backup/

├── security/

└── cloud/
```

Infrastructure should remain independent from application code.

============================================================
CONFIGURATION
============================================================

```text
config/

│

├── environments/

├── application/

├── authentication/

├── database/

├── ai/

├── logging/

├── monitoring/

└── feature-flags/
```

Configuration should never contain secrets.

============================================================
AUTOMATION
============================================================

```text
scripts/

│

├── build/

├── deploy/

├── migrate/

├── backup/

├── testing/

├── documentation/

└── maintenance/
```

Scripts should automate repetitive work.

============================================================
PROJECT PRINCIPLES
============================================================

Every folder should:

Have one responsibility.

Be logically named.

Avoid duplication.

Support scalability.

Remain documented.

============================================================
FOLDER RULES
============================================================

Never:

Mix unrelated files.

Store temporary files.

Duplicate components.

Create undocumented folders.

Break architecture.

Folder structure should remain stable.

============================================================
FINAL PRINCIPLE
============================================================

A well-organized project is easier to understand,

easier to maintain,

easier to scale,

and easier for future developers and AI systems to navigate.

The project structure should communicate the architecture before anyone reads the code.

============================================================
END OF PROJECT_TREE

============================================================
